### ðŸŒ´ What *Is* Palm Oil?

**Palm oil** is a type of **vegetable oil** derived from the **fruit of the oil palm tree**, specifically *Elaeis guineensis*. Itâ€™s *not* from the tree trunkâ€”itâ€™s from the **red, fleshy fruit** that grows in bunches near the top of the tree.

There are **two** main oils:
- **Palm oil** â€“ from the **fruitâ€™s flesh**
- **Palm kernel oil** â€“ from the **seed inside the fruit**

---

### ðŸ§ª Why Is Palm Oil Used So Much?

- **Long shelf life** (it resists oxidation)
- **Solid at room temp** (good for spreads, pastries, etc.)
- **Very cheap** to produce (high yield per acre)
- **Smooth texture** (great mouthfeel in processed foods)

Thatâ€™s why it ends up in everything from peanut butter to shampoo.

---

### âš ï¸ Health + Ethical Considerations

#### Health:
- **Unrefined palm oil** (red palm oil) has antioxidants like vitamin E and carotenoids.
- **Refined palm oil** (most common) is more neutral but often ultra-processed.
- High in **saturated fat**, so not ideal in large quantitiesâ€”but not evil either, especially if balanced with whole foods.

#### Ethics:
- **Deforestation** (especially in Indonesia & Malaysia)
- **Habitat destruction** (for orangutans and other species)

Thereâ€™s growing demand for **RSPO-certified** (sustainable) palm oilâ€”but you have to check labels or company claims to be sure.
